<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Item 8.01</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Other Events.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">On December 16, 2016, Intel Corporation announced that the upside trigger on its 2.95% Junior Subordinated Convertible Debentures Due 2035 (CUSIP No. 458140AD2)&#160;has been met&#160;for the six-month interest payment period from December 15, 2016 to June 15, 2017. As a result, contingent interest of approximately $4 million in the aggregate will be paid on the notes for that six-month interest payment period.</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The company's press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K.</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.95pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.95pt">Intel's 2.95% Junior Subordinated Convertible Debentures Due 2035</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.95pt">to Pay Contingent Interest of $4 Million</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">SANTA CLARA, Calif., Dec. 16, 2016 </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8211;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt"> Intel Corporation announced that the upside trigger on its 2.95 percent junior subordinated convertible debentures, which were issued in 2005 and are due 2035 (CUSIP No. 458140AD2) (the "Notes"), has been met for the six-month interest payment period from Dec. 15, 2016 to June 15, 2017. As a result, contingent interest will be paid on the Notes for that six-month interest payment period. Contingent interest of approximately $4 million in the aggregate on the $1.6 billion outstanding principal amount of the Notes, or approximately $2.50 per $1,000 principal amount of the Notes, will be paid on June 15, 2017, to the holders of record as of June 1, 2017.</font></div>

<br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">About Intel</div>

<div style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Intel (NASDAQ: INTC) expands the boundaries of technology to make the most amazing experiences possible. Information about Intel can be found at </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">newsroom.intel.com</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt"> and </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">intel.com</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 24.6pt">&#8211; 30 &#8211;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt">Intel and the Intel logo are trademarks of Intel Corporation in the United States and other countries.</div>
